collaboration , global issues , opensource , peace , politics , social media , violence , war	合作、全球性議題、資源開放、和平、政治、社交媒體、暴力、戰爭
james stavridis: how nato's supreme commander thinks about global security	詹姆士斯•斯塔弗里迪斯:北約組織的最高指揮官如何看待全球安全 。
i'm gonna talk a little bit about opensource security , because we've got to get better at security in this 21st century .	我將要談一些開放資源的安全性 , 因為我們必須在21世紀的安全方面做得更好 。
let me start by saying , let's look back to the 20th century , and kind of get a sense of how that style of security worked for us .	讓我先回顧一下20世紀 , 然後有點像是安全風格對我們來說是怎樣的 。
this is verdun , a battlefield in france just north of the nato headquarters in belgium .	這是verdun , 一個法國的戰場 , 就在北約在比利時總部的北邊 。
at verdun , in 1916 , over a 300day period , 700 , 000 people were killed , so about 2 , 000 a day .	在1916年的verdun這個活動 , 超過300天的期間 , 70萬人被殺害 , 所以大約每一天有2000人被殺 。
if you roll it forward 20thcentury security into the second world war , you see the battle of stalingrad , 300 days , 2 million people killed .	如果再向前推進二十世紀的安全 , 進入第二次世界大戰 , 你看到在斯大林格勒的抗爭 , 300天內 , 2000萬人死亡 。
we go into the cold war , and we continue to try and build walls .	我們進入冷戰 , 繼續建造圍牆 。
we go from the trench warfare of the first world war to the maginot line of the second world war , and then we go into the cold war , the iron curtain , the berlin wall .	我們從一戰的壕溝 , 到第二次世界大戰的馬基提防線 , 再到冷戰的鐵幕 , 柏林牆 。
my thesis for us today is , instead of building walls to create security , we need to build bridges .	我今天的主題是 , 與其建牆不如去創造安全 , 我們要造橋 。
this is a famous bridge in europe .	這是歐洲一座著名的橋
it's the bridge over the drina river , the subject of a novel by ivo andrić , and it talks about how , in that very troubled part of europe and the balkans , over time there's been enormous building of walls .	是drina河上方的橋 , ivoandrio的小說的主題 , 裡面談到在歐洲和巴爾幹地區 , 歐洲和巴爾幹地區 , 如何經過一段時間 , 建立了巨大的牆 。
more recently , in the last decade , we begin to see these communities start , hesitatingly , to come together .	更近期 , 在過去十年 , 我們開始看到這些社區開始 , 猶豫著 , 要團結在一起 。
i would argue , again , opensource security is about connecting the international , the interagency , the privatepublic , and lashing it together with strategic communication , largely in social networks .	我想再次重申 , 開放式安全是關乎國際的 , 跨部門的 , 私人的和公共的 , 並與戰略溝通聯繫在一起 。 主要是在社交網上 。
so let me talk a little bit about why we need to do that , because our global commons is under attack in a variety of ways , and none of the sources of threat to the global commons will be solved by building walls .	所以 , 讓我來談談為什麼我們需要這麼做 , 因為我們的全球公有物受到各種方式的攻擊 , 沒有威脅到全球公有物的來源 , 會透過築牆來解決 。
now , i'm a sailor , obviously .	現在 , 我當然是個水手 ,
this is a ship , a liner , clipping through the indian ocean .	這是一艘船 , 一艘拖船 , 穿過印度洋.
what's wrong with this picture ?	這張照片有什麼問題 ?
it's got concertina wire along the sides of it .	它的側邊有鋼索 。
that's to prevent pirates from attacking it .	也就是防止海盜襲擊
piracy is a very active threat today around the world . this is in the indian ocean .	海盜是當今全世界都很活躍的威脅 。 這是在印度洋 。
piracy is also very active in the strait of malacca .	在馬拉卡海盜也很活躍 。
it's active in the gulf of guinea .	在幾內亞灣
we see it in the caribbean .	我們看到在加勒比海
it's a $10billionayear discontinuity in the global transport system .	在全球交通運輸系統中 , 每隔一百億美金的損失 ,
last year , at this time , there were 20 vessels , 500 mariners held hostage .	去年 , 在這個時期 , 有20艘船 , 500名船員被挾持人質 。
this is an attack on the global commons .	這是對全球公有物的攻擊 。
we need to think about how to address it .	我們需要考慮如何解決
let's shift to a different kind of sea , the cyber sea .	讓我們轉到另一種海洋 , 網絡的海洋 。
here are photographs of two young men .	這裡有兩個年輕人的照片 。
at the moment , they're incarcerated .	在當下 , 他們被監禁在
they conducted a credit card fraud that netted them over 10 billion dollars .	他們進行了一個信用卡詐騙案 , 線上投入超過一百億美元 。
this is part of cybercrime which is a $2trillionayear discontinuity in the global economy .	這是網路犯罪的一部分 , 是全球經濟兩萬億美元的不連續性 。
two trillion a year .	每年兩兆 。
that's just under the gdp of great britain .	那只是英國的國內生產總值 。
so this cyber sea , which we know endlessly is the fundamental piece of radical openness , is very much under threat as well .	所以 , 我們所知的網路海 , 無止境地是激進開放的基本元素 , 也正受到威脅 。
another thing i worry about in the global commons is the threat posed by trafficking , by the movement of narcotics , opium , here coming out of afghanistan through europe over to the united states .	在全球公有物上 , 我擔心的另一件事就是販賣、麻醉劑、鴉片這些威脅 , 從阿富汗穿過歐洲到美國 。
we worry about cocaine coming from the andean ridge north .	我們擔心從andeanridge北部運過來的可卡因 。
we worry about the movement of illegal weapons and trafficking . above all , perhaps , we worry about human trafficking , and the awful cost of it .	我們擔心非法武器的運輸 。 最重要的是 , 我們擔心人口販賣 , 以及它的可怕代價 。
trafficking moves largely at sea but in other parts of the global commons .	販賣行為主要是在海上移動 , 但在全球公有物的其他部分 。
this is a photograph , and i wish i could tell you that this is a very hightech piece of us navy gear that we're using to stop the trafficking .	這是張照片 , 我希望我能告訴各位 , 這是非常高科技的美國海軍設備 , 我們用它來阻止人口販賣 。
the bad news is , this is a semisubmersible run by drug cartels .	壞消息是 , 這是一個販毒集團的半潛水器 。
it was built in the jungles of south america .	建在南美洲叢林中的
we caught it with that lowtech raft — — and it was carrying six tons of cocaine .	我們用低科技的木筏逮到它 , 它帶著六噸的可卡因 。
crew of four . sophisticated communications sweep .	四個船員 , 精良的溝通都掃了起來
this kind of trafficking , in narcotics , in humans , in weapons , god forbid , in weapons of mass destruction , is part of the threat to the global commons .	這種運輸 , 在毒品領域 , 人、武器、被禁止的運輸 , 在大規模毀滅性武器中 , 上帝是造成全球公有物威脅的一部分 。
and let's pull it together in afghanistan today .	並且讓我們今天一起在阿富汗 。
this is a field of poppies in afghanistan .	這是在阿富汗的一個熱鬧的領域
eighty to 90 percent of the world's poppy , opium and heroin , comes out of afghanistan .	全世界80%到90%的鍋子 , 鴉片和海洛因來自阿富汗 。
we also see there , of course , terrorism .	當然 , 我們也看到恐怖主義 。
this is where al qaeda is staged from .	這是基地組織的發源地 。
we also see a very strong insurgency embedded there .	我們也看到了一場強烈的暴動發生在那兒 。
so this terrorism concern is also part of the global commons , and what we must address .	所以 , 這種恐怖主義的擔憂也是全球公有物的一部分 , 也是我們必須要處理的 。
so here we are , 21st century .	所以 , 在21世紀 ,
we know our 20thcentury tools are not going to work .	我們知道我們20世紀的工具是行不通的
what should we do ?	我們應該怎麼做 ?
i would argue that we will not deliver security solely from the barrel of a gun .	我認為 , 我們不會僅僅依靠槍支來遞送安全性 。
we will not deliver security solely from the barrel of a gun .	我們不會僅僅依靠槍支來遞送安全 。
we will need the application of military force .	我們會需要軍事力量的應用 。
when we do it , we must do it well , and competently .	當我們這麼做時 , 我們必須要做得很好 , 且要有能力 。
but my thesis is , opensource security is about international , interagency , privatepublic connection pulled together by this idea of strategic communication on the internet .	但我的論點是 , 開放式安全是關于國際的 , 跨部門的 , 私人和公共的聯系 , 通過網際網路上的戰略性溝通而聯繫在一起 。
let me give you a couple of examples of how this works in a positive way .	讓我舉幾個例子 , 讓你們知道這是如何運作的 。
this is afghanistan . these are afghan soldiers .	這是阿富汗 。 這些是阿富汗士兵 。
they are all holding books .	他們都拿著書 。
you should say , " that's odd . i thought i read that this demographic , young men and women in their 20s and 30s , is largely illiterate in afghanistan . "	你應該說 , " 這太奇怪了 , 我以為我讀到過了這樣的人口分類學 , 20到30多歲的年輕人 , 在阿富汗是不識字的 。 "
you would be correct .	你是對的 。
eightyfive percent cannot read when they enter the security forces of afghanistan .	85%不識字 , 當他們進入阿富汗的安全部隊時 ,
why ? because the taliban withheld education during the period of time in which these men and women would have learned to read .	為什麼呢 ? 因為在這些男人和女人學會讀書的期間 , 塔利班都接受了教育 。
so the question is , so , why are they all standing there holding books ?	所以 , 問題是 , 為什麼他們都站在那裡拿書 ?
the answer is , we are teaching them to read in literacy courses by nato in partnership with private sector entities , in partnership with development agencies .	答案是 , 我們在北約與私人機構合作的課程中教導他們閱讀 , 與發展機構合作 。
we've taught well over 200 , 000 afghan security forces to read and write at a basic level .	我們已經教了超過20萬的阿富汗安全部隊以最基本的層次來讀和寫 。
when you can read and write in afghanistan , you will typically put a pen in your pocket .	當你能讀和寫在阿富汗時 , 通常就會放支筆在口袋裡 。
at the ceremonies , when these young men and women graduate , they take that pen with great pride , and put it in their pocket .	在畢業典禮上 , 當這些年輕的男女畢業 , 帶著驕傲的筆 , 把筆放進他們的口袋 。
this is bringing together international — there are 50 nations involved in this mission — interagency — these development agencies — and privatepublic , to take on this kind of security .	這讓國際組織起來 , 有五十個國家參與了這個項目 , 跨部門的合作開發部門 , 和公私部門 , 共同承擔安全的責任 。
now , we are also teaching them combat skills , of course , but i would argue , opensource security means connecting in ways that create longer lasting security effect .	當然 , 我們也在教他們格鬥技巧 , 但我會說 , 開放式安全意味著一種能創造更長久安全感的方式 。
this is a us navy warship .	這是美國海軍戰艦 。
it's called the comfort .	叫做舒適感 。
there's a sister ship called the mercy .	有一艘姊妹船 , 叫做mercy號 。
they are hospital ships .	他們是醫院的船隻 。
this one , the comfort , operates throughout the caribbean and the coast of south america conducting patient treatments .	這一個 , 舒適 , 在加勒比海和南美洲的海岸進行病人的治療 。
on a typical cruise , they'll do 400 , 000 patient treatments .	在一般的巡迴演出 , 他們會進行40萬次治療 。
it is crewed not strictly by military but by a combination of humanitarian organizations: operation hope , project smile .	船員不是嚴格的通過軍事行動 , 而是通過結合人道組織:運行希望、微笑的計劃 。
other organizations send volunteers .	其他組織送來志願者
interagency physicians come out .	各國的醫師會出面
they're all part of this .	他們都是這其中的一部分 。
to give you one example of the impact this can have , this little boy , eight years old , walked with his mother two days to come to the eye clinic put on by the comfort .	舉個例子來說 , 這個小男孩 , 八歲 , 和他的母親走了兩天來到安慰號上的眼科診所 。
when he was fitted , over his extremely myopic eyes , he suddenly looked up and said , " mama , veo el mundo . "	當他被裝備好時 , 透過他極端的微笑眼睛 , 他突然抬起頭 , 說: 「 媽媽 , veoelmundo 。 」
" mom , i see the world . "	「 媽媽 , 我看到世界了 。 」
multiply this by 400 , 000 patient treatments , this privatepublic collaboration with security forces , and you begin to see the power of creating security in a very different way .	把這個乘以4000000個病人治療 , 這個私人和公共的合作 , 通過安全力量的合作 , 你開始看見創造安全的力量 , 以一個非常不同的方式 。
here you see baseball players .	這裡你看到棒球選手
can you pick out the two us army soldiers in this photograph ?	你能從這張照片中挑出兩名美軍士兵嗎 ?
they are the two young men on either side of these young boys . this is part of a series of baseball clinics , where we have explored collaboration between major league baseball , the department of state , who sets up the diplomatic piece of this , military baseball players , who are real soldiers with real skills but participate in this mission , and they put on clinics throughout latin america and the caribbean , in honduras , in nicaragua , in all of the central american and caribbean nations where baseball is so popular , and it creates security .	他們是這群小男孩兩邊的小伙子 。 這是一系列棒球診所的成員 , 在那裡 , 我們一起探索了棒球大聯盟 , 國務院 , 設立了外交部門 , 軍隊棒球選手 , 他們是真正的軍人 , 用的是真正的技能 , 但他們參與了這項任務 , 把診所開到了拉丁美洲和加勒比海 , 開到了宏都拉斯 , 開到了塞拉瓜 , 開到了所有中美洲和加拉瓜 , 在這裡 , 創造了所有中美洲的流感 。
it shows role models to young men and women about fitness and about life that i would argue help create security for us .	它向年輕男女展現榜樣 , 關於體良以及生命的重要性 , 我主張幫我們創造安全 。
another aspect of this partnership is in disaster relief .	這種合作的另一方面在災難應變中
this is a us air force helicopter participating after the tsunami in 2004 which killed 250 , 000 people .	這是一架美國空軍的直升機 , 參與2004年海嘯後 , 造成25萬人死亡 。
in each of these major disasters — the tsunami in 2004 , 250 , 000 dead , the kashmiri earthquake in pakistan , 2005 , 85 , 000 dead , the haitian earthquake , about 300 , 000 dead , more recently the awful earthquaketsunami combination which struck japan and its nuclear industry — in all of these instances , we see partnerships between international actors , interagency , privatepublic working with security forces to respond to this kind of natural disaster .	在每一個重大災難中2004年的海嘯 , 25萬死 , 2005年巴基斯坦的喀什米爾地震 , 85000死 , 8000死 , 海地震 , 30萬人的死亡 , 最近則是令人難以置信的地震災害聯合體擊垮了日本和其核工業 。 在所有這些例子中 , 我們看到了國際間的合作夥伴 , 私有部門的合作關係 。
so these are examples of this idea of opensource security .	所以這些就是開放式安全的例子
we tie it together , increasingly , by doing things like this .	我們將它綁得越來越緊 , 做成這樣的東西 。
now , you're looking at this thinking , " ah , admiral , these must be sea lanes of communication , or these might be fiber optic cables . "	現在 , 你看到的這個是想: 「 啊 , 沒道理 , 這些一定是通信交流的海道 , 或者這些是光纖電纜 。 」
no . this is a graphic of the world according to twitter .	不 。 這張圖是根據推特推出的世界 。
purple are tweets . green are geolocation .	紫色是推特 。 綠色是地點 。
white is the synthesis .	白色是合成的
it's a perfect evocation of that great population survey , the six largest nations in the world in descending order: china , india , facebook , the united states , twitter and indonesia .	這是很棒的人口調查中 , 六大國家依次排名下降:中國、印度、臉書、美國、推特 , 和印尼 。
why do we want to get in these nets ?	我們為什麼要買這些漁網呢 ?
why do we want to be involved ?	我們為什麼想要參與其中呢 ?
we talked earlier about the arab spring , and the power of all this .	我們之前談到阿拉伯之春 , 以及這一切的力量 。
i'll give you another example , and it's how you move this message .	我再舉一個例子 , 就是你如何移動這個訊息 。
i gave a talk like this in london a while back about this point . i said , as i say to all of you , i'm on facebook . friend me .	我在倫敦發表一場像這樣子的演講 。 我跟你們說 , 我在facebook上 , 請親愛的 。
got a little laugh from the audience .	觀眾笑了起來 。
there was an article which was run by ap , on the wire .	曾經有一篇文章 , ap , 在電線上執行 。
got picked up in two places in the world: finland and indonesia .	被帶到世界上兩個地方:芬蘭和印尼
the headline was: nato admiral needs friends .	標題是:北大西洋公約需要朋友們
and the story was a catalyst , and the next morning i had hundreds of facebook friend requests from indonesians and finns , mostly saying , " admiral , we heard you need a friend , and oh , by the way , what is nato ? "	故事是一名催化劑第二天早上我就有上百個facebook好友請求 , 來自印尼和芬蘭多數人請求 , 主要是說: 「 司令傳 , 我們聽說你需要一個朋友 , 喔 , 順帶一提 , nato是甚麼 ? 」
yeah , we laugh , but this is how we move the message , and moving that message is how we connect international , interagency , privatepublic , and these social nets to help create security .	是啊 , 我們笑了 , 但這是我們如何移動訊息 , 移動那個訊息就是我們如何連結國際 , 跨部門 , 私人和公共的 , 還有這些社群網絡 , 來協助創造安全 。
now , let me hit a somber note .	現在 , 讓我嚴肅地說 ,
this is a photograph of a brave british soldier .	這張照片是一位勇敢的英國士兵 。
he's in the scots guards .	他在蘇格蘭衛隊
he's standing the watch in helmand , in southern afghanistan .	他正站在helmand , 在阿富汗南部 ,
i put him here to remind us , i would not want anyone to leave the room thinking that we do not need capable , competent militaries who can create real military effect .	我把他放到這裡來提醒我們 , 我不希望有人離開房間 , 認為我們不需要能夠創造真正的軍事力量 。
that is the core of who we are and what we do , and we do it to protect freedom , freedom of speech , all the things we treasure in our societies .	那就是我們是誰以及我們做什麼的核心我們為了保護自由 , 言論自由和所有我們在社會中珍視的東西
but , you know , life is not an onandoff switch .	但是 , 你知道 , 生命不是一個開關 。
you don't have to have a military that is either in hard combat or is in the barracks .	不用在戰鬥中的軍隊 , 也不用在兵營裡 。
i would argue life is a rheostat .	我會說 , 人生是個混亂者 。
you have to dial it in , and as i think about how we create security in this 21st century , there will be times when we will apply hard power in true war and crisis , but there will be many instances , as we've talked about today , where our militaries can be part of creating 21stcentury security , international , interagency , privatepublic , connected with competent communication .	你必須調一個數值 , 並且正如我所想的我們在21世紀裡如何創造安全 , 將有一些時候我們在真正的戰爭和危機中運用硬實力 , 但是會有很多的例子 , 正如我們今天所談到的 , 我們的軍隊可以成為21世紀安全的一部分 , 國際的 , 跨部門的 , 公私的 , 與溝通聯繫在一起的力量 。
i would close by saying that we heard earlier today about wikipedia . i use wikipedia all the time to look up facts , and as all of you appreciate , wikipedia is not created by 12 brilliant people locked in a room writing articles .	我最後想說的是 , 今天早些時候聽到的就是維基百科 。 我經常使用維基百科查一些事實 , 正如你們所有人都很欣賞維基百科 , 不是靠12個聰明的人把自己關在房間裡寫文章來創作 。
wikipedia , every day , is tens of thousands of people inputting information , and every day millions of people withdrawing that information .	維基百科 , 每天有數萬人輸入資訊 , 每天都有數百萬人在報導這些資訊 。
it's a perfect image for the fundamental point that no one of us is as smart as all of us thinking together .	這是個完美的圖像 , 可以說明我們當中沒有任何人是那麼聰明的 , 就跟我們所有人一起思考的一樣 。
no one person , no one alliance , no one nation , no one of us is as smart as all of us thinking together .	沒有一個人 , 沒有一個聯盟 , 沒有一個國家 , 像我們所有人一起思考一樣聰明 。
the vision statement of wikipedia is very simple: a world in which every human being can freely share in the sum of all knowledge .	維基百科的宣言很簡單:一個每個人可以自由共享所有知識的世界 。
my thesis for you is that by combining international , interagency , privatepublic , strategic communication , together , in this 21st century , we can create the sum of all security .	我的論點是 , 藉由結合國際 , 跨部門 , 公私的 , 戰略通信 , 一起在21世紀 , 我們能創造出安全的總和 。
thank you very much . thank you . thank you .	非常感謝 。 謝謝 。
